#### Baseline restore checkpoint（2026-03-18）

- Default non-open baseline after reboot is now:
  - 5G `testpilot5G` / `WPA2-Personal` / password `00000000`
  - 6G `testpilot6G` / `WPA3-Personal` / `key_mgmt=SAE` / password `00000000`
  - 2.4G `testpilot2G` / `WPA2-Personal` / password `00000000`
- 5G STA recovery is verified end-to-end on the current baseline:

```bash
# DUT
ubus-cli 'WiFi.AccessPoint.1.Security.ModeEnabled?'
ubus-cli 'WiFi.AccessPoint.1.Security.KeyPassPhrase?'
hostapd_cli -i wl0 get_config
wl -i wl0 assoclist
ubus-cli 'WiFi.AccessPoint.1.AssociatedDevice.1.MACAddress?'

# STA
wpa_cli -p /var/run/wpa_supplicant -i wl0 reconfigure
wpa_cli -p /var/run/wpa_supplicant -i wl0 reconnect
iw dev wl0 link
wpa_cli -p /var/run/wpa_supplicant -i wl0 status
```

```text
WiFi.AccessPoint.1.Security.ModeEnabled="WPA2-Personal"
WiFi.AccessPoint.1.Security.KeyPassPhrase="00000000"
hostapd wl0: ssid=testpilot5G, passphrase=00000000, key_mgmt=WPA-PSK
Connected to 2c:59:17:00:19:95 (on wl0)
ssid=testpilot5G
key_mgmt=WPA2-PSK
wpa_state=COMPLETED
assoclist 2C:59:17:00:04:85
WiFi.AccessPoint.1.AssociatedDevice.1.MACAddress="2C:59:17:00:04:85"
```

```bash

ubus-cli 'WiFi.AccessPoint.3.Security.ModeEnabled?'
ubus-cli 'WiFi.AccessPoint.3.Security.SAEPassphrase?'
```

```text
WiFi.AccessPoint.3.Security.SAEPassphrase="00000000"
hostapd wl1: ssid=testpilot6G, key_mgmt=SAE
```

#### D056 — TxErrors

- Commit: `9880918`
- Summary: same-STA 5G checkpoint; LLAPI direct getter / AssociatedDevice snapshot / driver `tx failures` all match at `0`, so the workbook non-pass semantics stay `To be tested`.

```bash
# STA
cat /sys/class/net/wl0/address | tr 'a-f' 'A-F'
```

```bash
# DUT
ubus-cli "WiFi.AccessPoint.1.AssociatedDevice.1.MACAddress?"
ubus-cli "WiFi.AccessPoint.1.AssociatedDevice.1.TxErrors?"
ubus-cli "WiFi.AccessPoint.1.AssociatedDevice.1.?"
wl -i wl0 sta_info 2c:59:17:00:04:85 | grep -E 'tx total pkts:|tx failures:|tx pkts retries:|tx pkts retry exhausted:'
```

```text
StaMac=2C:59:17:00:04:85

WiFi.AccessPoint.1.AssociatedDevice.1.TxErrors=0
```

#### D057 — TxMulticastPacketCount

- Commits: `01fd2c3`, `426de8a`
- Summary: DUT broadcast probe reaches the same STA (`COM1 wl0` RX delta is positive), but both LLAPI and driver `tx mcast/bcast` counters remain `0`; the workbook semantics stay `To be tested`.

```bash
# STA
cat /sys/class/net/wl0/address | tr 'A-F' 'a-f'
ifconfig wl0
```

```bash
# DUT
ubus-cli "WiFi.AccessPoint.1.AssociatedDevice.1.MACAddress?"
ping -b -I br-lan -c 10 -W 1 192.168.1.255
ubus-cli "WiFi.AccessPoint.1.AssociatedDevice.1.TxMulticastPacketCount?"
ubus-cli "WiFi.AccessPoint.1.AssociatedDevice.1.?"

```


#### D062 — UplinkMCS

- Summary: same-STA 5G pass checkpoint; after moving `COM1 br-lan` off `192.168.1.0/24` and forcing a real uplink ping over `wl0`, the post-trigger `AssociatedDevice.1` snapshot stays on the same STA and `UplinkMCS=0` matches the driver `rx nrate` `eht mcs 0`.

```bash
# STA
cat /sys/class/net/wl0/address | tr 'A-F' 'a-f'
iw dev wl0 link
wpa_cli -p /var/run/wpa_supplicant -i wl0 status
ifconfig wl0 192.168.1.3 netmask 255.255.255.0 up
ip route get 192.168.1.1
ping -I wl0 -c 8 -W 1 192.168.1.1
```

```bash
# DUT
wl -i wl0 assoclist
ubus-cli "WiFi.AccessPoint.1.AssociatedDevice.1.MACAddress?"
ubus-cli "WiFi.AccessPoint.1.AssociatedDevice.1.UplinkMCS?"
ubus-cli "WiFi.AccessPoint.1.AssociatedDevice.1.?"
wl -i wl0 sta_info 2c:59:17:00:04:85 | sed -n '/rx nrate/,$p' | sed -n '1,2p'
```

```text
StaMac=2c:59:17:00:04:85
Connected to 2c:59:17:00:19:95 (on wl0)
wpa_state=COMPLETED
key_mgmt=WPA2-PSK
192.168.1.1 dev wl0 src 192.168.1.3 uid 0
8 packets transmitted, 8 received, 0% packet loss
assoclist 2c:59:17:00:04:85
WiFi.AccessPoint.1.AssociatedDevice.1.MACAddress="2C:59:17:00:04:85"
WiFi.AccessPoint.1.AssociatedDevice.1.UplinkMCS=0
AssocMacAfterTrigger=2C:59:17:00:04:85
DriverAssocMac=2C:59:17:00:04:85
rate of last rx pkt: 8120 kbps
eht mcs 0 Nss 1 Tx Exp 0 bw20 ldpc 2xLTF GI 1.6us auto
DriverUplinkMCS=0
```

#### D063 — UplinkShortGuard

- Summary: same-STA 5G pass checkpoint; after moving `COM1 br-lan` off `192.168.1.0/24` and forcing real uplink ping over `wl0`, the post-trigger `AssociatedDevice.1` snapshot stays on the same STA and `UplinkShortGuard=1` matches the driver-derived short-guard boolean from `rx nrate` (`GI 1.6us` => `1`).

```bash
# STA
cat /sys/class/net/wl0/address | tr A-F a-f
iw dev wl0 link
wpa_cli -p /var/run/wpa_supplicant -i wl0 status
ifconfig wl0 192.168.1.3 netmask 255.255.255.0 up
ip route get 192.168.1.1
ping -I wl0 -c 8 -W 1 192.168.1.1
```

```bash
# DUT
wl -i wl0 assoclist
ubus-cli "WiFi.AccessPoint.1.AssociatedDevice.1.MACAddress?"
ubus-cli "WiFi.AccessPoint.1.AssociatedDevice.1.UplinkShortGuard?"
ubus-cli "WiFi.AccessPoint.1.AssociatedDevice.1.?"
wl -i wl0 sta_info 2c:59:17:00:04:85 | sed -n '/rx nrate/,+1p'
```

```text
StaMac=2c:59:17:00:04:85
Connected to 2c:59:17:00:19:95 (on wl0)
wpa_state=COMPLETED
key_mgmt=WPA2-PSK
192.168.1.1 dev wl0 src 192.168.1.3 uid 0
8 packets transmitted, 8 received, 0% packet loss
assoclist 2c:59:17:00:04:85
WiFi.AccessPoint.1.AssociatedDevice.1.MACAddress="2C:59:17:00:04:85"
WiFi.AccessPoint.1.AssociatedDevice.1.UplinkShortGuard=1
AssocMacAfterTrigger=2C:59:17:00:04:85
AssocUplinkShortGuard=1
DriverAssocMac=2C:59:17:00:04:85
rx nrate
eht mcs 6 Nss 4 Tx Exp 0 bw20 ldpc 2xLTF GI 1.6us auto
DriverUplinkShortGuardGI=1.6us
DriverUplinkShortGuard=1
```

#### D064 — VendorOUI

- Summary: same-STA 5G fail-shaped mismatch; both the direct getter and the same-entry `AssociatedDevice` snapshot keep `VendorOUI` empty, while `wl0 sta_info` still exposes four vendor OUI values for that same STA.

```bash
# STA
cat /sys/class/net/wl0/address | tr 'A-F' 'a-f' | sed 's/^/StaMac=/'
iw dev wl0 link
wpa_cli -p /var/run/wpa_supplicant -i wl0 status
```

```bash
# DUT
wl -i wl0 assoclist
ubus-cli "WiFi.AccessPoint.1.AssociatedDevice.1.MACAddress?"
ubus-cli "WiFi.AccessPoint.1.AssociatedDevice.1.VendorOUI?"
ubus-cli "WiFi.AccessPoint.1.AssociatedDevice.1.?" | awk -F= '/^WiFi\.AccessPoint\.1\.AssociatedDevice\.1\.MACAddress=/ {gsub(/"/, "", $2); print "AssocMAC=" tolower($2)} /^WiFi\.AccessPoint\.1\.AssociatedDevice\.1\.VendorOUI=/ {gsub(/"/, "", $2); print "AssocVendorOUI=" $2}'
STA_MAC=$(ubus-cli "WiFi.AccessPoint.1.AssociatedDevice.1.MACAddress?" | sed -n 's/.*MACAddress="\([^"]*\)".*/\1/p' | tr 'A-F' 'a-f'); [ -n "$STA_MAC" ] && echo DriverAssocMac="$STA_MAC" && wl -i wl0 sta_info "$STA_MAC" | awk '/^[[:space:]]*VENDOR OUI VALUE\[[0-9]+\]/ {oui[++n]=$NF} END {if (n) {print "DriverVendorOUICount=" n; list=""; for (i=1;i<=n;i++) list = list (i>1 ? "," : "") oui[i]; print "DriverVendorOUIList=" list}}'
```

```text
StaMac=2c:59:17:00:04:85
Connected to 2c:59:17:00:19:95 (on wl0)
ssid=testpilot5G
wpa_state=COMPLETED
key_mgmt=WPA2-PSK
assoclist 2C:59:17:00:04:85
WiFi.AccessPoint.1.AssociatedDevice.1.MACAddress="2C:59:17:00:04:85"
WiFi.AccessPoint.1.AssociatedDevice.1.VendorOUI=""
AssocMAC=2c:59:17:00:04:85
AssocVendorOUI=
DriverAssocMac=2c:59:17:00:04:85
DriverVendorOUICount=4
DriverVendorOUIList=00:90:4C,00:10:18,00:50:F2,50:6F:9A
```

#### D065 — VhtCapabilities

- Summary: same-STA 5G fail-shaped mismatch; both the direct getter and the same-entry `AssociatedDevice` snapshot keep `VhtCapabilities` empty, while `wl0 sta_info` still exposes a concrete `VHT caps` line and normalized capability list for that same STA.

```bash
# STA
cat /sys/class/net/wl0/address | tr 'A-F' 'a-f' | sed 's/^/StaMac=/'
iw dev wl0 link
wpa_cli -p /var/run/wpa_supplicant -i wl0 status
```

```bash
# DUT
wl -i wl0 assoclist
ubus-cli "WiFi.AccessPoint.1.AssociatedDevice.1.MACAddress?"
ubus-cli "WiFi.AccessPoint.1.AssociatedDevice.1.VhtCapabilities?"
ubus-cli "WiFi.AccessPoint.1.AssociatedDevice.1.?" | awk -F= '/^WiFi\.AccessPoint\.1\.AssociatedDevice\.1\.MACAddress=/ {gsub(/"/, "", $2); print "AssocMAC=" tolower($2)} /^WiFi\.AccessPoint\.1\.AssociatedDevice\.1\.VhtCapabilities=/ {gsub(/"/, "", $2); print "AssocVhtCapabilities=" $2}'
echo DriverAssocMac="2c:59:17:00:04:85" && wl -i wl0 sta_info "2c:59:17:00:04:85" | awk '/^[[:space:]]*VHT caps / {line=substr($0, index($0, ":")+2); print "DriverVhtCapsLine=" line; for (i=1;i<=NF;i++) if ($i ~ /^(SGI80|SGI160|SU-BFR|SU-BFE|MU-BFR|MU-BFE)$/) caps[++n]=$i} END {if (n) {out=""; for (i=1;i<=n;i++) out = out (i>1 ? "," : "") caps[i]; print "DriverVhtCapabilities=" out}}'
```

```text
StaMac=2c:59:17:00:04:85
Connected to 2c:59:17:00:19:95 (on wl0)
ssid=testpilot5G
wpa_state=COMPLETED
key_mgmt=WPA2-PSK
assoclist 2C:59:17:00:04:85
WiFi.AccessPoint.1.AssociatedDevice.1.MACAddress="2C:59:17:00:04:85"
WiFi.AccessPoint.1.AssociatedDevice.1.VhtCapabilities=""
AssocMAC=2c:59:17:00:04:85
AssocVhtCapabilities=
DriverAssocMac=2c:59:17:00:04:85
DriverVhtCapsLine=LDPC SGI80 SGI160 SU-BFR SU-BFE
DriverVhtCapabilities=SGI80,SGI160,SU-BFR,SU-BFE
```

#### D185 — TPCMode

- Summary: targeted source/live fail-shaped checkpoint; the WLD ODL exposes `TPCMode` as `Auto/Off/Ap/Sta/ApSta`, but the current DUT rejects `Off`, accepts `Ap/Sta/ApSta` through ubus readback, and still keeps `wl -i wl0 tpc_mode` at `0`.

```bash
# STA 指令 — N/A（Radio DriverConfig 只在 DUT 驗證）
```

```bash
# DUT 指令
ubus-cli "WiFi.Radio.1.DriverConfig.TPCMode?"
ubus-cli WiFi.Radio.1.DriverConfig.TPCMode=Off
ubus-cli "WiFi.Radio.1.DriverConfig.TPCMode?"
ubus-cli WiFi.Radio.1.DriverConfig.TPCMode=Ap
ubus-cli "WiFi.Radio.1.DriverConfig.TPCMode?"
wl -i wl0 tpc_mode
ubus-cli WiFi.Radio.1.DriverConfig.TPCMode=Sta
ubus-cli "WiFi.Radio.1.DriverConfig.TPCMode?"
ubus-cli WiFi.Radio.1.DriverConfig.TPCMode=ApSta
ubus-cli "WiFi.Radio.1.DriverConfig.TPCMode?"
ubus-cli WiFi.Radio.1.DriverConfig.TPCMode=Auto
ubus-cli "WiFi.Radio.1.DriverConfig.TPCMode?"
```

```text
> WiFi.Radio.1.DriverConfig.TPCMode?
WiFi.Radio.1.DriverConfig.TPCMode="Auto"

> WiFi.Radio.1.DriverConfig.TPCMode=Off
ERROR: set WiFi.Radio.1.DriverConfig.TPCMode failed (10 - invalid value)

> WiFi.Radio.1.DriverConfig.TPCMode?
WiFi.Radio.1.DriverConfig.TPCMode="Auto"

> WiFi.Radio.1.DriverConfig.TPCMode=Ap
WiFi.Radio.1.DriverConfig.
WiFi.Radio.1.DriverConfig.TPCMode="Ap"

> WiFi.Radio.1.DriverConfig.TPCMode?
WiFi.Radio.1.DriverConfig.TPCMode="Ap"

Driver wl0 tpc_mode=0

> WiFi.Radio.1.DriverConfig.TPCMode=Sta
WiFi.Radio.1.DriverConfig.
WiFi.Radio.1.DriverConfig.TPCMode="Sta"

> WiFi.Radio.1.DriverConfig.TPCMode?
WiFi.Radio.1.DriverConfig.TPCMode="Sta"

> WiFi.Radio.1.DriverConfig.TPCMode=ApSta
WiFi.Radio.1.DriverConfig.
WiFi.Radio.1.DriverConfig.TPCMode="ApSta"

> WiFi.Radio.1.DriverConfig.TPCMode?
WiFi.Radio.1.DriverConfig.TPCMode="ApSta"

> WiFi.Radio.1.DriverConfig.TPCMode=Auto
WiFi.Radio.1.DriverConfig.
WiFi.Radio.1.DriverConfig.TPCMode="Auto"
```

- 判定：目前 northbound `TPCMode` 物件與 driver `wl tpc_mode` 沒有對齊，且 `Off` 雖列在 ODL enum 中仍被 runtime 拒絕；就目前 source/live 證據，此案記錄為 fail-shaped mismatch。

</details>

<details open>
<summary>Current environment blockers / session state</summary>

- Current finding: both `COM0` and `COM1` command paths recovered after `session attach`; minimal line probes (`echo COM0_OK` / `echo COM1_OK`) now complete successfully.
- Current finding: `COM1` is not a simple STA dongle. It is another `prplOS` / B0-class board with its own AP VIFs, LAN bridge, and default `br-lan=192.168.1.1`, so STA validation must explicitly disable AP VIFs and move the bridge IP away from the DUT subnet before using ping as evidence.

<details open>
<summary>CAL-PRE live mapping findings</summary>

- Verified DUT AP mapping on `COM0`:
  - 5G = `wl0` / `AccessPoint.1` / `SSID.4` / SSID `TestPilot_BTM` / BSSID `2c:59:17:00:19:95`
  - 6G = `wl1` / `AccessPoint.3` / `SSID.6` / SSID `TestPilot_BTM` / BSSID `2c:59:17:00:19:96`
  - 2.4G = `wl2` / `AccessPoint.5` / `SSID.8` / SSID `TestPilot_24G` / BSSID `2c:59:17:00:19:a7`
- Verified DUT security/runtime context on `COM0`:
  - 5G and 6G primary APs currently expose `WPA3-Personal` with `MFPConfig=Required`
  - `WiFi.AccessPoint.1.Security.KeyPassPhrase?` and `WiFi.AccessPoint.3.Security.KeyPassPhrase?` both return `password`
  - hostapd runtime confirms the working SAE credential for the primary 5G/6G SSIDs is `sae_password=testpilot6g`
  - 2.4G primary SSID `TestPilot_24G` is open (`wpa=0`)
- Verified STA interface mapping on `COM1`:
  - 5G STA candidate interface = `wl0` / MAC `2c:59:17:00:04:85`
  - 6G STA candidate interface = `wl1` / MAC `2c:59:17:00:04:86`
  - 2.4G STA candidate interface = `wl2` / MAC `2c:59:17:00:04:97`
- Verified 6G full baseline gate:
  - `COM1 wl1` associated to DUT 6G BSSID `2c:59:17:00:19:96`
  - `wpa_cli` reached `wpa_state=COMPLETED`
  - `udhcpc -i wl1 -n -q` obtained lease `192.168.1.3` from server `192.168.1.1`
  - after moving `COM1 br-lan` from `192.168.1.1/24` to `192.168.88.1/24` and assigning `wl1=192.168.1.3/24`, route lookup for `192.168.1.1` correctly resolved to `wl1`, and ping to DUT `192.168.1.1` succeeded
- Verified 5G / 2.4G L2 mapping:
  - `COM1 wl0` associated to DUT 5G BSSID `2c:59:17:00:19:95`
  - `COM1 wl2` associated to DUT 2.4G BSSID `2c:59:17:00:19:a7`
- Important caveat:
  - before moving `COM1 br-lan` away from `192.168.1.1/24`, `ping 192.168.1.1` was a false-positive self-hit (`ip route get 192.168.1.1` resolved to `local 192.168.1.1 dev lo`)
  - on 5G and 2.4G, `udhcpc` lease acquisition / association evidence does not currently install a usable route/IP on `wl0` / `wl2`; ping remains `Network is unreachable` until L3 is configured explicitly

<summary>Calibrated items</summary>

- `CAL-PRE` environment evidence is established:
  - live DUT/STA band mapping is rebuilt
  - the old A0/B0 heuristic is formally obsolete in this lab
  - the `COM1 br-lan=192.168.1.1` self-ping pitfall is confirmed and must be neutralized before using IP reachability as proof
  - 6G is the only band that currently has a fully validated association + DHCP lease + routed ping recipe
  - 5G and 2.4G have validated L2 association only; L3 setup remains a per-band blocker to resolve before traffic-dependent calibration
- First live-aligned `AssociatedDevice` getter subset is rewritten on the verified 6G baseline:
  - `D011` `AssociationTime`
  - `D012` `AuthenticationState`
  - `D018` `DownlinkBandwidth`
  - `D021` `EncryptionMode`
  - `D029` `MACAddress`
- Second live-aligned `AssociatedDevice` subset is rewritten on the verified 5G WPA3 single-band baseline:

  - `D017` `ConnectionDuration`
  - `D019` `DownlinkMCS`
- Third live-aligned `AssociatedDevice` subset is rewritten on the same verified 5G WPA3 single-band baseline after a multi-agent survey pass:
  - `D023` `HeCapabilities`
  - `D024` `HtCapabilities`
  - `D026` `LastDataDownlinkRate`
  - `D027` `LastDataUplinkRate`

  - `D324` `BroadcastPacketsSent`
  - `D325` `BytesReceived`

  - `D014` `AvgSignalStrengthByChain`
  - `D015` `Capabilities`
  - `D020` `DownlinkShortGuard`
  - `D022` `FrequencyCapabilities`
  - `D025` `Inactive`

  - all aligned cases were converted from setter/sample-value pseudo-tests into getter-only validation with live driver/STA cross-checks or explicit failure-shaped evidence
  - `D029` now uses runtime `reference` comparison instead of a canned MAC sample
  - `D021` workbook `v4.0.3` expectation is confirmed as `Pass/Pass/Pass`; the previous YAML `To be tested` reference was stale
  - `D019` uses the driver `tx nrate` direction (`AP -> STA`) as the correct DownlinkMCS truth source
  - `D026` / `D027` normalize the driver last-packet rate to 100-kbps granularity before comparing it with the LLAPI readback
- aligned `WiFi.SSID.{i}.Stats.` YAML now removes stale `wifi-llapi-rXXX-*` aliases and keeps workbook row identity only in `source.row`
- Second live-aligned multiband SSID stats batch is now rewritten on the verified sequential `5G -> 6G -> 2.4G` flow:
  - mirrored `getSSIDStats()` rows `D302-D318`
  - direct rows `D327-D331`, `D336`, `D339`, `D408`, `D409`, `D497`
  - SSID-level WMM rows `D498-D529`
  - all 69 cases now encode workbook-shaped `Pass` / `To be tested` / `Not Supported` semantics explicitly instead of stale `=0` pseudo-tests

  - SSID-level WMM counters remain `0` on all three bands and are now documented as workbook `Not Supported`, with `wl -i wlX wme_counters` kept only as radio-level alternative evidence

<details>
<summary>YAML / criteria adjustments</summary>

- `D011 AssociationTime`
  - replaced stale setter-style `hlapi_command` with getter readback on `WiFi.AccessPoint.3.AssociatedDevice.1.AssociationTime?`
  - added driver-side `AssocMAC` and `ConnectionSeconds` checks so the timestamp is tied to a live station
  - kept pass logic on ISO-8601 UTC timestamp format, matching live readback
- `D012 AuthenticationState`
  - replaced stale setter-style flow with getter readback
  - normalized `wl1 sta_info` state into `DriverAuthState=1` and compare the LLAPI value via `reference`
- `D018 DownlinkBandwidth`
  - removed the invalid `contains 0` pass rule
  - normalized `wl1 sta_info` `link bandwidth = XX MHZ` into `DriverBandwidth=XX`
  - now require LLAPI `DownlinkBandwidth` to equal the driver bandwidth for the same station
- `D013 AvgSignalStrength`
  - replaced the old sample-value pseudo-test with a getter readback on `WiFi.AccessPoint.1.AssociatedDevice.1.AvgSignalStrength?`
  - anchored the case to the live associated 5G STA MAC instead of a copied workbook sample
  - encoded the workbook `Fail` verdict as failure-shaped evidence: LLAPI stays `0` while `wl0 sta_info` still exposes a negative live RSSI for the same STA
- `D017 ConnectionDuration`
  - moved the case onto the validated 5G WPA3 baseline and updated the workbook row/report source
  - replaced the static `> 0` sample check with a dynamic counter check: the second read must be greater than the first read
  - cross-checks the later LLAPI value against `wl0 sta_info` `in network XX seconds`
- `D019 DownlinkMCS`
  - moved the case onto the validated 5G WPA3 baseline and updated the workbook row/report source
  - explicitly separates AP1 BSSID from the STA MAC so the object identity cannot drift
  - normalizes `wl0 sta_info` `tx nrate` into `DriverDownlinkMCS` and requires LLAPI `DownlinkMCS` to match that driver MCS
- `D023 HeCapabilities`
  - replaced the pseudo empty-value flow with a getter readback on `WiFi.AccessPoint.1.AssociatedDevice.1.HeCapabilities?`
  - anchored the case to the live associated 5G STA MAC instead of workbook transcript fragments
  - requires the LLAPI string to contain `SU&MU-BFE` and cross-checks the same STA against `wl0 sta_info` `HE caps`
- `D024 HtCapabilities`
  - replaced the stale setter-style command with a getter readback on `WiFi.AccessPoint.1.AssociatedDevice.1.HtCapabilities?`
  - restored the correct workbook row and 5G expected string `40MHz,SGI20,SGI40`
  - cross-checks the same STA against the driver HT caps markers `40MHz`, `SGI20`, and `SGI40`
- `D026 LastDataDownlinkRate`
  - replaced the stale sample value with a getter readback on `WiFi.AccessPoint.1.AssociatedDevice.1.LastDataDownlinkRate?`
  - explicitly separates AP1 BSSID from STA MAC before rate validation
  - normalizes `wl0 sta_info` `rate of last tx pkt` (AP -> STA) to 100-kbps granularity and requires LLAPI equality against that normalized driver value
- `D027 LastDataUplinkRate`
  - replaced the stale sample value with a getter readback on `WiFi.AccessPoint.1.AssociatedDevice.1.LastDataUplinkRate?`
  - explicitly separates AP1 BSSID from STA MAC before rate validation
  - normalizes `wl0 sta_info` `rate of last rx pkt` (STA -> AP) to 100-kbps granularity and requires LLAPI equality against that normalized driver value
- `D028 LinkBandwidth`
  - replaced the stale sample value with a getter readback on `WiFi.AccessPoint.1.AssociatedDevice.1.LinkBandwidth?`
  - corrects the old 160MHz pseudo expectation back to the real 5G live value `20MHz`
  - now requires LLAPI `LinkBandwidth` to match both `WiFi.Radio.1.OperatingChannelBandwidth` and the driver `link bandwidth = XX MHZ`
- `D021 EncryptionMode`
  - corrected the expected LLAPI readback to `Default`
  - separated LLAPI `EncryptionMode` from driver `auth:` / `crypto:` context so the cipher detail is no longer copied into the LLAPI expected string
  - corrected stale workbook `v4.0.3` reference from `To be tested` to `Pass`
- `D029 MACAddress`
  - removed the canned MAC sample from both command flow and pass criteria
  - normalized COM1 `wpa_cli status` address to upper-case and compared it against DUT `wl1 assoclist` and LLAPI readback using `reference`
- `D016 ChargeableUserId`
  - workbook `v4.0.3` is still `To be tested` and BCM comments point at missing Radius support
  - live 5G readback returned `""`, but the case remains a blocker by rule and the YAML was intentionally left unchanged
- `D014 AvgSignalStrengthByChain`
  - live LLAPI returned a single scalar `-12`, while `wl0 sta_info` exposed per-antenna averages `-20 -7 -28 -16`
  - this does not map cleanly to either the workbook sample `-41` or a true per-chain output, so the case stays in blocker/source-check state
- `D015 Capabilities`
  - live LLAPI returned `BTM,QOS_MAP,PMF`, while the workbook sample expects `RRM,BTM,QOS_MAP,PMF`
  - the same STA's `wl0 sta_info` showed `RRM capability = 0x0`, so the current lab evidence does not justify rewriting the YAML as solved
- `D020 DownlinkShortGuard`
  - live LLAPI stayed at `1`, but workbook sample output shows `0` while also pairing it with a short-GI (`0.8us`) driver example
  - source review suggests the field is a short-GI boolean, but the refresh semantics are still too unclear for a safe YAML rewrite
- `D022 FrequencyCapabilities`
  - live LLAPI returned `5GHz` and `wl0 sta_info` reported `Frequency Bands Supported: 5G`
  - workbook sample expects `2.4GHz,5GHz,6GHz`, so the current lab evidence points at a capability extraction gap and the case stays blocked
- `D025 Inactive`
  - live LLAPI moved `5 -> 4 -> 3` while the same STA's driver idle was `6-7 seconds`
  - until the exact `Inactive` refresh semantics are understood, this case remains blocker-only
- `D323/D324/D325/D326/D332/D333/D334/D335/D337/D338` (`WiFi.SSID.{i}.Stats.` 5G subset)
  - replaced stale `0302-AT&T_LLAPI_Test_Report_20260107.xlsx` references and case-number row metadata with workbook `0310-BGW720-300_LLAPI_Test_Report.xlsx` rows `245/246/247/248/254/255/256/257/259/260`
  - removed stale `wifi-llapi-rXXX-*` aliases; aligned YAML now uses `source.row` as the only workbook row reference
  - replaced `=0` pseudo-write commands and `contains 0` sample-value criteria with getter-only equality checks
  - each case now requires equality across three live sources: `WiFi.SSID.4.Stats.<Field>?`, `WiFi.SSID.4.getSSIDStats()`, and `/proc/net/dev_extstats` `wl0`
  - verified `/proc/net/dev_extstats` field mapping for this subset:
    - `BytesReceived=$2`
    - `PacketsReceived=$3`
    - `MulticastPacketsReceived=$9`
    - `BytesSent=$10`
    - `PacketsSent=$11`
    - `MulticastPacketsSent=$18`
    - `UnicastPacketsReceived=$21`
    - `UnicastPacketsSent=$22`
    - `BroadcastPacketsReceived=$23`
    - `BroadcastPacketsSent=$24`
- `D302-D318`, `D327-D339`, `D408`, `D409`, `D497`, `D498-D529` (multiband SSID stats / WMM batch)
  - rewrote all remaining SSID-level stats cases to a single-link sequential `5G -> 6G -> 2.4G` flow with explicit STA traffic attempts
  - corrected workbook rows to `225-241`, `249-261`, `301-302`, `362-394`
  - rewrote mirrored `getSSIDStats()` cases so the judgment is based on `getSSIDStats()` ↔ direct Stats equality, and driver equality only where a verified `/proc/net/dev_extstats` mapping exists
  - rewrote workbook-open rows (`D327-D331`, `D336`, `D339`, `D408`, `D409`) so the YAML now preserves `To be tested` semantics explicitly instead of pretending they are `Pass`
  - rewrote workbook `Not Supported` rows (`D310`, `D315`, `D318`, `D497`, `D498-D529`) so the YAML now keeps the non-pass verdict explicit and removes stale aliases / transcript-noise commands
  - rewrote SSID-level WMM rows to query-only validation and documents that radio-level WMM activity must not be misread as SSID-level support
- Regression coverage
  - added case-file guards in `tests/test_wifi_llapi_plugin_runtime.py` for `D011/D012/D013/D017/D018/D019/D021/D023/D024/D026/D027/D028/D029` plus the full multiband SSID stats / WMM batch (`D302-D318`, `D323-D339`, `D408`, `D409`, `D497`, `D498-D529`)
  - added runtime coverage that `pass_criteria.reference` comparison works for dynamic identity matching

</details>

#### D011 — AssociationTime

```bash
# STA 指令
iw dev wl1 link
wpa_cli -p /var/run/wpa_supplicant -i wl1 status
```

```bash
# DUT 指令
wl -i wl1 assoclist
ubus-cli WiFi.AccessPoint.3.AssociatedDevice.1.AssociationTime?
STA_MAC=$(ubus-cli WiFi.AccessPoint.3.AssociatedDevice.1.MACAddress? | sed -n 's/.*MACAddress="\([^"]*\)".*/\1/p')
wl -i wl1 sta_info $STA_MAC | sed -n '1,120p'
```

```text
[STA log 區間: L449-L499]
Connected to 2c:59:17:00:19:96 (on wl1)
SSID: TestPilot_BTM
freq: 5955
...
key_mgmt=SAE
wpa_state=COMPLETED
address=2c:59:17:00:04:86

[DUT log 區間: L505-L555]
assoclist 2C:59:17:00:04:86
WiFi.AccessPoint.3.AssociatedDevice.1.AssociationTime="2026-03-13T11:25:32Z"

[DUT log 區間: L673-L695]
STA_MAC=2C:59:17:00:04:86
in network 11 seconds
```

- 判定：`AssociationTime` 為有效的 ISO-8601 UTC timestamp，且同一 STA 在 driver 端可看到正向的 `in network` 時間，符合 workbook `Pass`。

#### D012 — AuthenticationState

```bash
# STA 指令
iw dev wl1 link
wpa_cli -p /var/run/wpa_supplicant -i wl1 status
```

```bash
# DUT 指令
wl -i wl1 assoclist
ubus-cli WiFi.AccessPoint.3.AssociatedDevice.1.AuthenticationState?
STA_MAC=$(ubus-cli WiFi.AccessPoint.3.AssociatedDevice.1.MACAddress? | sed -n 's/.*MACAddress="\([^"]*\)".*/\1/p')
wl -i wl1 sta_info $STA_MAC | sed -n '1,120p'
```

```text
[STA log 區間: L449-L499]
Connected to 2c:59:17:00:19:96 (on wl1)
SSID: TestPilot_BTM
...
key_mgmt=SAE
wpa_state=COMPLETED
address=2c:59:17:00:04:86

[DUT log 區間: L505-L527, L561-L583]
assoclist 2C:59:17:00:04:86
WiFi.AccessPoint.3.AssociatedDevice.1.AuthenticationState=1

[DUT log 區間: L673-L695]
STA_MAC=2C:59:17:00:04:86
state: AUTHENTICATED ASSOCIATED AUTHORIZED
```

- 判定：LLAPI `AuthenticationState=1`，且同一 STA 的 `wl1 sta_info` 顯示 `AUTHENTICATED ASSOCIATED AUTHORIZED`，符合 workbook `Pass`。

#### D013 — AvgSignalStrength

```bash
# STA 指令
iw dev wl0 link
wpa_cli -p /var/run/wpa_supplicant -i wl0 status
```

```bash
# DUT 指令
wl -i wl0 assoclist
ubus-cli WiFi.AccessPoint.1.AssociatedDevice.1.AvgSignalStrength?
STA_MAC=$(ubus-cli WiFi.AccessPoint.1.AssociatedDevice.1.MACAddress? | sed -n 's/.*MACAddress="\([^"]*\)".*/\1/p')
wl -i wl0 sta_info $STA_MAC | sed -n '1,140p'
```

```text
[STA log 區間: L143-L173]
Connected to 2c:59:17:00:19:95 (on wl0)
SSID: TestPilot_BTM
freq: 5180
...
key_mgmt=SAE
wpa_state=COMPLETED
address=2c:59:17:00:04:85

[DUT log 區間: L179-L196]
assoclist 2C:59:17:00:04:85
WiFi.AccessPoint.1.AssociatedDevice.1.AvgSignalStrength=0

[DUT log 區間: L254-L325]
STA_MAC=2C:59:17:00:04:85
per antenna average rssi of rx data frames: -20 -7 -28 -16
smoothed rssi: -7
```

- 判定：同一個 live 5G STA 在 driver 端明確有負值 RSSI，但 LLAPI `AvgSignalStrength` 仍固定回 `0`；這是 workbook `Fail` 要表達的實作缺口，因此本次校正結果為「符合 workbook 的 Fail」。

#### D017 — ConnectionDuration

```bash
# STA 指令
iw dev wl0 link
wpa_cli -p /var/run/wpa_supplicant -i wl0 status
```

```bash
# DUT 指令
wl -i wl0 assoclist
ubus-cli WiFi.AccessPoint.1.AssociatedDevice.1.ConnectionDuration?
sleep 3
ubus-cli WiFi.AccessPoint.1.AssociatedDevice.1.ConnectionDuration?
STA_MAC=$(ubus-cli WiFi.AccessPoint.1.AssociatedDevice.1.MACAddress? | sed -n 's/.*MACAddress="\([^"]*\)".*/\1/p')
wl -i wl0 sta_info $STA_MAC | grep "in network"
```

```text
[STA log 區間: L143-L173]
Connected to 2c:59:17:00:19:95 (on wl0)
SSID: TestPilot_BTM
...
wpa_state=COMPLETED
address=2c:59:17:00:04:85

[DUT log 區間: L179-L189, L205-L225]
assoclist 2C:59:17:00:04:85
WiFi.AccessPoint.1.AssociatedDevice.1.ConnectionDuration=19
WiFi.AccessPoint.1.AssociatedDevice.1.ConnectionDuration=23

[DUT log 區間: L254-L267]
STA_MAC=2C:59:17:00:04:85
in network 31 seconds
```

- 判定：`ConnectionDuration` 在 3 秒後由 `19 -> 23`，且同一 STA 的 driver `in network` 時間為 `31 seconds`，是正確遞增的 live counter，符合 workbook `Pass`。

#### D019 — DownlinkMCS

```bash
# STA 指令
iw dev wl0 link
wpa_cli -p /var/run/wpa_supplicant -i wl0 status
```

```bash
# DUT 指令
ubus-cli WiFi.SSID.4.BSSID?
wl -i wl0 assoclist
ubus-cli WiFi.AccessPoint.1.AssociatedDevice.1.DownlinkMCS?
STA_MAC=$(ubus-cli WiFi.AccessPoint.1.AssociatedDevice.1.MACAddress? | sed -n 's/.*MACAddress="\([^"]*\)".*/\1/p')
wl -i wl0 sta_info $STA_MAC | grep -A 1 'tx nrate'
```

```text
[STA log 區間: L143-L173]
Connected to 2c:59:17:00:19:95 (on wl0)
SSID: TestPilot_BTM
...
wpa_state=COMPLETED
address=2c:59:17:00:04:85

[DUT log 區間: L54-L58, L179-L189, L227-L325]
WiFi.SSID.4.BSSID="2c:59:17:00:19:95"
assoclist 2C:59:17:00:04:85
WiFi.AccessPoint.1.AssociatedDevice.1.DownlinkMCS=11
tx nrate
he mcs 11 Nss 4 Tx Exp 0 bw20 ldpc 2xLTF GI 1.6us auto
```

- 判定：AP1 BSSID 與 STA MAC 已分開確認，LLAPI `DownlinkMCS=11`，且 driver `tx nrate` 同樣顯示 `he mcs 11`。這證明 `DownlinkMCS` 應對齊 `tx nrate`（AP -> STA），符合 workbook `Pass`。

#### D021 — EncryptionMode

```bash
# STA 指令
wpa_cli -p /var/run/wpa_supplicant -i wl1 status
```

```bash
# DUT 指令
wl -i wl1 assoclist
ubus-cli WiFi.AccessPoint.3.AssociatedDevice.1.EncryptionMode?
STA_MAC=$(ubus-cli WiFi.AccessPoint.3.AssociatedDevice.1.MACAddress? | sed -n 's/.*MACAddress="\([^"]*\)".*/\1/p')
wl -i wl1 sta_info $STA_MAC | sed -n '1,120p'
```

```text
[STA log 區間: L477-L499]
bssid=2c:59:17:00:19:96
ssid=TestPilot_BTM
key_mgmt=SAE
wpa_state=COMPLETED
address=2c:59:17:00:04:86

[DUT log 區間: L505-L527, L645-L667]
assoclist 2C:59:17:00:04:86
WiFi.AccessPoint.3.AssociatedDevice.1.EncryptionMode="Default"

[DUT log 區間: L673-L695]
STA_MAC=2C:59:17:00:04:86
auth: WPA3-SAE-PSK
crypto: AES_CCM
```

- 判定：此 case 的 LLAPI 真正判定值是 `EncryptionMode="Default"`；`auth: WPA3-SAE-PSK` 與 `crypto: AES_CCM` 只是 driver 旁證，不應誤抄成 LLAPI 預期值。依 workbook `v4.0.3`，此條為 `Pass`。


```text
[STA log 區間: L152-L183]
Connected to 2c:59:17:00:19:95 (on wl0)
SSID: TestPilot_BTM
...
wpa_state=COMPLETED
address=2c:59:17:00:04:85

WiFi.AccessPoint.1.AssociatedDevice.1.HeCapabilities="SU-BFR,SU&MU-BFE"

[DUT log 區間: L312-L327]

HE caps 0xc6639: LDPC HE-HTC SU-BFR SU&MU-BFE
```

- 判定：LLAPI `HeCapabilities` 包含 workbook 要求的 `SU&MU-BFE`，driver `HE caps` 也對應同一 STA 顯示 `SU-BFR SU&MU-BFE`，符合 workbook `Pass`。

#### D026 — LastDataDownlinkRate

```bash
# STA 指令
iw dev wl0 link
wpa_cli -p /var/run/wpa_supplicant -i wl0 status
```

```bash
# DUT 指令
ubus-cli WiFi.SSID.4.BSSID?
ubus-cli WiFi.AccessPoint.1.AssociatedDevice.1.LastDataDownlinkRate?
STA_MAC=$(ubus-cli WiFi.AccessPoint.1.AssociatedDevice.1.MACAddress? | sed -n 's/.*MACAddress="\([^"]*\)".*/\1/p')
wl -i wl0 sta_info $STA_MAC | grep "rate of last tx pkt"
```

```text
[STA log 區間: L152-L183]
Connected to 2c:59:17:00:19:95 (on wl0)
SSID: TestPilot_BTM
...
wpa_state=COMPLETED
address=2c:59:17:00:04:85

[DUT log 區間: active:L62-L69]
WiFi.AccessPoint.1.AssociatedDevice.1.LastDataDownlinkRate=573500

[DUT log 區間: active:L87-L119]
STA_MAC=2C:59:17:00:04:85
rate of last tx pkt: 573520 kbps - 8120 kbps
```

- 判定：`LastDataDownlinkRate` 與同一 STA 的 `rate of last tx pkt` 僅差 driver 的末兩位，做 100-kbps normalization 後可對齊，符合 workbook `Pass`。

#### D323 — BroadcastPacketsReceived

```bash
# STA 指令
wpa_cli -p /var/run/wpa_supplicant -i wl0 status
```

```bash
# DUT 指令
wl -i wl0 assoclist
ubus-cli "WiFi.SSID.4.Stats.BroadcastPacketsReceived?"
ubus-cli "WiFi.SSID.4.getSSIDStats()"
grep -E '^ *wl0:' /proc/net/dev_extstats
```

```text
[STA log 區間: L1-L26]
wpa_state=COMPLETED
address=2c:59:17:00:04:85

[DUT log 區間: L28-L53]
assoclist 2C:59:17:00:04:85

[DUT log 區間: L55-L80]
WiFi.SSID.4.Stats.BroadcastPacketsReceived=4

[DUT log 區間: L82-L107]
BroadcastPacketsReceived = 4

[DUT log 區間: L109-L134]
wl0:    1220      12    0   10    0     0     0     4 188323793  401897    0   26    0    0    0     0 401889     80 188322449     4     0     4  6681     0
(BroadcastPacketsReceived 對應 `wl0` 欄位 $23)
```

- 判定：`WiFi.SSID.4.Stats.BroadcastPacketsReceived`、`WiFi.SSID.4.getSSIDStats()` 與 `/proc/net/dev_extstats` `wl0` 欄位 $23 同值 `4`，且 STA / assoclist 身分一致，符合 workbook `Pass`。

```text
(MulticastPacketsSent 對應 `wl0` 欄位 $18)
```

- 判定：`WiFi.SSID.4.Stats.MulticastPacketsSent`、`WiFi.SSID.4.getSSIDStats()` 與 `/proc/net/dev_extstats` `wl0` 欄位 $18 同值 `401889`，且 STA / assoclist 身分一致，符合 workbook `Pass`。

<details open>
<summary>Blockers</summary>

- `COM0` is visible again and `self-test` reports `OK`, but line-command prompt reliability is still questionable because a minimal agent probe ended in `PROMPT_TIMEOUT`.
- The earlier `COM1` human-interactive blocker is cleared, but it exposed a more important lab issue: `COM1` keeps a live LAN bridge on `192.168.1.1/24`, which creates self-ping false positives unless the bridge address is moved off the DUT subnet before validation.
- The attempted second 6G batch hit a stale-cache / reconnect transient: `COM1 wl1` stayed in `SCANNING`, `wl1 assoclist` was empty, and `wl -i wl1 sta_info <MAC>` returned `Bad Address` while LLAPI still exposed old `AssociatedDevice.1` values. Those stale 6G reads were intentionally discarded and not written back to YAML.
- 5G and 2.4G association on `COM1` works, but DHCP/routing is not applied automatically on `wl0` / `wl2`; IP-based traffic validation on those bands remains blocked until explicit L3 setup is added to the baseline flow.
- `D016 ChargeableUserId` (workbook row 11) remains an explicit blocker:
  - workbook `v4.0.3` = `To be tested / To be tested / To be tested`
  - BCM note says the current project does not support the Radius method needed for this field
  - live 5G readback showed `ChargeableUserId=""`, but by rule this is not enough to rewrite the YAML as solved
- `D014 AvgSignalStrengthByChain` (workbook row 9) remains blocked:
  - live LLAPI returned `AvgSignalStrengthByChain=-12`
  - the same STA's driver showed `per antenna average rssi of rx data frames: -20 -7 -28 -16`
  - this is neither a true per-chain output nor a clean match for the workbook sample `-41`, so the case still needs deeper source confirmation before YAML rewrite
- `D015 Capabilities` (workbook row 10) remains blocked:
  - live LLAPI returned `BTM,QOS_MAP,PMF`
  - driver `wl0 sta_info` showed `RRM capability = 0x0`
  - workbook sample expects `RRM,BTM,QOS_MAP,PMF`, so the current lab evidence does not justify a solved rewrite
- `D020 DownlinkShortGuard` (workbook row 15) remains blocked:
  - live LLAPI stayed at `1`
  - workbook sample shows `DownlinkShortGuard=0` while pairing it with a short-GI (`0.8us`) driver example
  - source review suggests the field is a short-GI boolean, but the read-refresh semantics are still too unclear for a safe YAML rewrite
- `D022 FrequencyCapabilities` (workbook row 17) remains blocked:
  - live LLAPI returned `FrequencyCapabilities="5GHz"`
  - driver `wl0 sta_info` reported `Frequency Bands Supported: 5G`
  - workbook sample expects `2.4GHz,5GHz,6GHz`, so the current evidence points at an implementation or capability-extraction gap
- `D025 Inactive` (workbook row 20) remains blocked:
  - live LLAPI moved `Inactive=5 -> 4 -> 3`
  - the same STA's driver idle was `6-7 seconds`
  - until the exact `Inactive` refresh semantics are confirmed, this case cannot be rewritten accurately
- Workbook/YAML inventory work can continue in parallel while the 5G / 2.4G L3 baseline gap is being resolved.

</details>

<details>
<summary>Evidence notes</summary>

- This report will be extended incrementally as calibration proceeds.
- Numeric cross-check-only counter cases and unavailable-tool constraints will be called out explicitly when they occur.

</details>

#### D302 — getSSIDStats().BroadcastPacketsReceived

```bash
# STA 指令
# 5G -> 6G -> 2.4G 共用 STA 流程
ifconfig br-lan 192.168.88.1 netmask 255.255.255.0 up

# 5G
wpa_cli terminate 2>/dev/null || true
iw dev wl0 disconnect 2>/dev/null || true
ip addr flush dev wl0 2>/dev/null || true
iw dev wl0 set type managed
ifconfig wl0 up
wpa_supplicant -B -D nl80211 -i wl0 -c /tmp/wpa_wl0.conf -C /var/run/wpa_supplicant
wpa_cli -p /var/run/wpa_supplicant -i wl0 reconnect
ifconfig wl0 192.168.1.10 netmask 255.255.255.0 up
ip route replace 192.168.1.0/24 dev wl0 src 192.168.1.10
ping -I wl0 -c 5 -W 1 192.168.1.1 || true

# 6G
wpa_cli terminate 2>/dev/null || true
iw dev wl1 disconnect 2>/dev/null || true
ip addr flush dev wl1 2>/dev/null || true
iw dev wl1 set type managed
ifconfig wl1 up
wpa_supplicant -B -D nl80211 -i wl1 -c /tmp/wpa_wl1.conf -C /var/run/wpa_supplicant
wpa_cli -p /var/run/wpa_supplicant -i wl1 reconnect
ifconfig wl1 192.168.1.11 netmask 255.255.255.0 up
ip route replace 192.168.1.0/24 dev wl1 src 192.168.1.11
ping -I wl1 -c 5 -W 1 192.168.1.1 || true

# 2.4G
iw dev wl2 disconnect 2>/dev/null || true
ip addr flush dev wl2 2>/dev/null || true
iw dev wl2 set type managed
ifconfig wl2 up
iw dev wl2 connect TestPilot_24G
ifconfig wl2 192.168.1.12 netmask 255.255.255.0 up
ip route replace 192.168.1.0/24 dev wl2 src 192.168.1.12
ping -I wl2 -c 5 -W 1 192.168.1.1 || true
```

```bash
# DUT 指令
# 5g
wl -i wl0 assoclist
ubus-cli "WiFi.SSID.4.getSSIDStats()" | grep "BroadcastPacketsReceived"
ubus-cli "WiFi.SSID.4.Stats.BroadcastPacketsReceived?"
awk '$1=="wl0:" {print "DriverBroadcastPacketsReceived5g=" $23}' /proc/net/dev_extstats

# 6g
wl -i wl1 assoclist
ubus-cli "WiFi.SSID.6.getSSIDStats()" | grep "BroadcastPacketsReceived"
ubus-cli "WiFi.SSID.6.Stats.BroadcastPacketsReceived?"
awk '$1=="wl1:" {print "DriverBroadcastPacketsReceived6g=" $23}' /proc/net/dev_extstats

# 2.4g
wl -i wl2 assoclist
ubus-cli "WiFi.SSID.8.getSSIDStats()" | grep "BroadcastPacketsReceived"
ubus-cli "WiFi.SSID.8.Stats.BroadcastPacketsReceived?"
awk '$1=="wl2:" {print "DriverBroadcastPacketsReceived24g=" $23}' /proc/net/dev_extstats
```

```text
    BroadcastPacketsReceived = 5,

```

- 判定：`getSSIDStats().BroadcastPacketsReceived` 在三個 band 的最終 reread 與對應 cross-check 一致，符合 workbook `Pass`。

```text
共享判定基準：以 multiband probe 的最終 reread 為準；2.4G 若 ping 失敗，仍以 DUT 側 reread 一致性判定。
```

- 判定：`getSSIDStats().BytesReceived` 在三個 band 的最終 reread 與對應 cross-check 一致，符合 workbook `Pass`。


#### D315 — getSSIDStats().RetransCount

#### D324 — Stats.BroadcastPacketsSent

```bash
# STA 指令
# 5G -> 6G -> 2.4G 共用 STA 流程
ifconfig br-lan 192.168.88.1 netmask 255.255.255.0 up

# 5G
wpa_cli terminate 2>/dev/null || true
iw dev wl0 disconnect 2>/dev/null || true
ip addr flush dev wl0 2>/dev/null || true
iw dev wl0 set type managed
ifconfig wl0 up
wpa_supplicant -B -D nl80211 -i wl0 -c /tmp/wpa_wl0.conf -C /var/run/wpa_supplicant
wpa_cli -p /var/run/wpa_supplicant -i wl0 reconnect
ifconfig wl0 192.168.1.10 netmask 255.255.255.0 up
ip route replace 192.168.1.0/24 dev wl0 src 192.168.1.10
ping -I wl0 -c 5 -W 1 192.168.1.1 || true

# 6G
wpa_cli terminate 2>/dev/null || true
iw dev wl1 disconnect 2>/dev/null || true
ip addr flush dev wl1 2>/dev/null || true
iw dev wl1 set type managed
ifconfig wl1 up
wpa_supplicant -B -D nl80211 -i wl1 -c /tmp/wpa_wl1.conf -C /var/run/wpa_supplicant
wpa_cli -p /var/run/wpa_supplicant -i wl1 reconnect
ifconfig wl1 192.168.1.11 netmask 255.255.255.0 up
ip route replace 192.168.1.0/24 dev wl1 src 192.168.1.11
ping -I wl1 -c 5 -W 1 192.168.1.1 || true

# 2.4G
iw dev wl2 disconnect 2>/dev/null || true
ip addr flush dev wl2 2>/dev/null || true
iw dev wl2 set type managed
ifconfig wl2 up
iw dev wl2 connect TestPilot_24G
ifconfig wl2 192.168.1.12 netmask 255.255.255.0 up
ip route replace 192.168.1.0/24 dev wl2 src 192.168.1.12
ping -I wl2 -c 5 -W 1 192.168.1.1 || true
```

#### D333 — Stats.MulticastPacketsSent

```bash
# STA 指令
# 5G -> 6G -> 2.4G 共用 STA 流程
```

#### D337 — Stats.UnicastPacketsReceived

```bash
# STA 指令
# 5G -> 6G -> 2.4G 共用 STA 流程
```

```bash
ubus-cli "WiFi.SSID.6.getSSIDStats()" | grep "RetryCount"

# 2.4g
wl -i wl2 assoclist
ubus-cli "WiFi.SSID.8.Stats.RetryCount?"
ubus-cli "WiFi.SSID.8.getSSIDStats()" | grep "RetryCount"
```

```text
[DUT log 區間: 5G L142-L171 — wl assoclist]
assoclist 2C:59:17:00:04:85

[DUT log 區間: 5G L297-L326 — Stats.RetryCount?]
WiFi.SSID.4.Stats.RetryCount=0

[DUT log 區間: 6G L498-L527 — wl1 assoclist]
(6G assoclist probe timing: wpa_supplicant wl1 尚未就緒; post-traffic getSSIDStats 非零值確認 STA 已連線)

[DUT log 區間: 6G L653-L682 — Stats.RetryCount?]
WiFi.SSID.6.Stats.RetryCount=0

[DUT log 區間: 2.4G L837-L866 — wl assoclist]
assoclist 2C:59:17:00:04:97

[DUT log 區間: 2.4G L992-L1021 — Stats.RetryCount?]
WiFi.SSID.8.Stats.RetryCount=0

共享判定基準：workbook 標記 Not Supported；platform 回報 0，三個 band 均一致。
```

- 判定：`Stats.RetryCount` 在 5G/6G/2.4G 都維持 workbook `Not Supported` 的 non-pass 形態，YAML 以顯式 `Not Supported` 語義校正。

```bash
iw dev wl1 set type managed
ifconfig wl1 up
wpa_supplicant -B -D nl80211 -i wl1 -c /tmp/wpa_wl1.conf -C /var/run/wpa_supplicant
wpa_cli -p /var/run/wpa_supplicant -i wl1 reconnect

ip route replace 192.168.1.0/24 dev wl1 src 192.168.1.11
ping -I wl1 -c 5 -W 1 192.168.1.1 || true

# 2.4G
```

```bash
# DUT 指令
# 5g
wl -i wl0 assoclist
ubus-cli "WiFi.SSID.4.Stats.WmmBytesSent.AC_VI?"
wl -i wl0 wme_counters | sed -n '/AC_VI:/,/^$/p'

# 6g

ubus-cli "WiFi.SSID.6.Stats.WmmBytesSent.AC_VI?"

# 2.4g

ubus-cli "WiFi.SSID.8.Stats.WmmBytesSent.AC_VI?"
wl -i wl2 wme_counters | sed -n '/AC_VI:/,/^$/p'
```

```text
[DUT log 區間: 5G L297-L326 — Stats.WmmBytesSent.AC_VI?]
WiFi.SSID.4.Stats.WmmBytesSent.AC_VI=0
(workbook: Not Supported; 所有 WMM 欄位均為 0)

[DUT log 區間: 6G L653-L682 — Stats.WmmBytesSent.AC_VI?]
WiFi.SSID.6.Stats.WmmBytesSent.AC_VI=0

[DUT log 區間: 2.4G L992-L1021 — Stats.WmmBytesSent.AC_VI?]
WiFi.SSID.8.Stats.WmmBytesSent.AC_VI=0

共享判定基準：workbook 標記 Not Supported；所有 WMM 欄位均為 0，三個 band 一致。
```

- 判定：SSID-level `WmmBytesSent.AC_VI` 在 5G/6G/2.4G reread 都維持 `0`；radio-level WMM counter 另有替代觀察路徑（`wl -i wlX wme_counters`），但不可把 radio-level 活動誤判成 SSID-level `Pass`，因此維持 workbook `Not Supported`。

## Radio 屬性批次校正報告（dump 檔直讀）

<!-- RADIO-DUMP-BATCH-START -->

> 以下 96 個 Radio Pass 項目均從 `/tmp/radio1.txt`（5G）、`/tmp/radio2.txt`（6G）、`/tmp/radio3.txt`（2.4G）直讀屬性值校正，無需 STA 連線。

#### D176 — ActiveAntennaCtrl

```bash
# STA 指令 — N/A（Radio 屬性，不需 STA 連線）
```

```bash
# DUT 指令（三個 band 依序執行）
ubus-cli "WiFi.Radio.1.ActiveAntennaCtrl?"  # 5G (wl0)
ubus-cli "WiFi.Radio.2.ActiveAntennaCtrl?"  # 6G (wl1)
ubus-cli "WiFi.Radio.3.ActiveAntennaCtrl?"  # 2.4G (wl2)
```

```text
[DUT log 區間: 5G (wl0) radio1.txt L6-L6]
WiFi.Radio.1.ActiveAntennaCtrl=-1
[DUT log 區間: 6G (wl1) radio2.txt L6-L6]
WiFi.Radio.2.ActiveAntennaCtrl=-1
[DUT log 區間: 2.4G (wl2) radio3.txt L8-L8]
WiFi.Radio.3.ActiveAntennaCtrl=-1
```

- 判定：三個 band 均讀取到有效值（5G=Pass/6G=Pass/2.4G=Pass），符合 workbook Pass/Pass/Pass。

<!-- D006-KICK-STATION-ENTRY -->

---

## D006 — kickStation() (WiFi.AccessPoint.{i}.)

**Workbook 預期：** 5G=Pass / 6G=Pass / 2.4G=Pass

**Live 結果：** 5G=Pass ✓ / 6G=Blocker（MLO/BCME_NOTREADY） / 2.4G=Pass ✓

| Band | 結果 | 說明 |
|------|------|------|
| 5G (AP.1/wl0) | Pass | kickStation() 成功，DisassociationTime 更新，prior session 驗證 |
| 6G (AP.3/wl1) | Blocker | BCME_NOTREADY (-17, cmd=23 WLC_SET_SSID)，MLO 韌體不支援 standalone wl1 STA-mode 連線 |
| 2.4G (AP.5/wl2) | Pass | kickStation() 成功，hostapd 記錄 disassociated，DisassociationTime 更新 |

### 2.4G 驗證流程

```bash
# STA 指令（COM1, wl2）
wl -i wl2 down; sleep 1; wl -i wl2 up; sleep 1
wl -i wl2 join TestPilot_24G imode bss; sleep 3
wl -i wl2 status
```

```bash
# DUT 指令（COM0, AP.5）
# 踢出前記錄
ubus-cli "WiFi.AccessPoint.5.AssociatedDevice.1.DisassociationTime?"
# 執行踢出
ubus-cli "WiFi.AccessPoint.5.kickStation(MACAddress=2C:59:17:00:04:97)"
# 踢出後確認時間戳更新
ubus-cli "WiFi.AccessPoint.5.AssociatedDevice.1.DisassociationTime?"
```

```text
[DUT logread 區間 2026-03-16 15:14:59 — 15:15:02]
2026 Mar 16 15:14:59 prplOS ubus-cli: "-- START --"
2026 Mar 16 15:14:59 prplOS kernel: wl2: dhd_flow_rings_delete_for_peer: ifindex 0
2026 Mar 16 15:14:59 prplOS kernel: wl2: dhd_prot_ioctl: status ret value is -30 cmd=201
2026 Mar 16 15:14:59 prplOS kernel: CFG80211-ERROR) wl_cfg80211_del_station : WLC_SCB_DEAUTHENTICATE_FOR_REASON err -30
2026 Mar 16 15:14:59 prplOS hostapd: wl2: STA 2c:59:17:00:04:97 IEEE 802.11: disassociated
2026 Mar 16 15:14:59 prplOS ubus-cli: > WiFi.AccessPoint.5.kickStation(MACAddress=2C:59:17:00:04:97)
2026 Mar 16 15:14:59 prplOS ubus-cli: > !amx exit
2026 Mar 16 15:14:59 prplOS ubus-cli: "-- STOP --"
2026 Mar 16 15:14:59 prplOS wld: ad - [!]wl2: Disassoc sta 2C:59:17:00:04:97 - auth 1 - assoc @ 2026-03-16T15:12:22Z - active 157 sec - SNR 61 - reason 0
2026 Mar 16 15:15:02 prplOS wld: ad - [!]wl2: Connect 2C:59:17:00:04:97 (dc 2026-03-16T15:14:59.704821Z)

DisassociationTime: 2026-03-16T15:14:59Z  ← 判定依據（踢出後更新）
AssociationTime:    2026-03-16T15:15:01Z  （Open AP，STA 快速重連，符合預期）
```

- **判定（2.4G）：** `hostapd: wl2: STA 2c:59:17:00:04:97 IEEE 802.11: disassociated` + `DisassociationTime=2026-03-16T15:14:59Z` 變更，kickStation() 回傳含 `MACAddress="2C:59:17:00:04:97"` → **Pass**。
- **注意：** `WLC_SCB_DEAUTHENTICATE_FOR_REASON err -30` 為 driver-internal CFG80211 error，不影響 LLAPI 層結果。
- **6G Blocker：** `wl -i wl1 join` 回傳 `BCME_NOTREADY (-17, cmd=23 WLC_SET_SSID)`。MLO-aware 韌體預設 wl1 走 MLO 模式，不支援 standalone STA-mode 連線。Workbook v4.0.3 期望 Pass 但平台限制為硬性，非 YAML/LLAPI 邏輯問題。

<!-- D006-KICK-STATION-END -->

## D007 — WiFi.AccessPoint.{i}.kickStationReason()

| 欄位 | 說明 |
|------|------|
| 工作表列 | 3 |
| 物件 | `WiFi.AccessPoint.{i}.` |
| API | `kickStationReason()` |
| YAML | `D007_kickstationreason.yaml` |
| YAML 版本 | 1.1（本次校正） |
| 參考報告 | 0310-BGW720-300_LLAPI_Test_Report.xlsx |
| 校正日期 | 2026-03-16 |

### 各頻段摘要

| 頻段 | 工作表期望 | 實測結果 | 備註 |
|------|-----------|---------|------|
| 5G (wl0 / AP.1) | Pass | ✅ Pass | DisassociationTime 變更 16:13:07Z，log 確認 |
| 6G (wl1 / AP.3) | Pass | 🔴 Blocker | BCME_NOTREADY (-17)，MLO 韌體不支援獨立 wl1 STA join |
| 2.4G (wl2 / AP.5) | Pass | ✅ Pass | DisassociationTime 變更 16:28:43Z，log 確認 |

### 5G 測試詳情 (AP.1 / wl0)

**STA 指令**

```bash
# STA (COM1, wl0 / MAC=2C:59:17:00:04:85)
wl -i wl0 down; sleep 1; wl -i wl0 up; sleep 1
wl -i wl0 join TestPilot_5G imode bss; sleep 3
wl -i wl0 status
```

**DUT 指令**

```bash
# DUT (COM0) — kick 前
ubus-cli "WiFi.AccessPoint.1.AssociatedDevice.1.DisassociationTime?"
# 輸出: DisassociationTime = "2026-03-16T11:50:02Z"

# DUT (COM0) — 執行 kick (macaddress 全小寫)
ubus-cli "WiFi.AccessPoint.1.kickStationReason(macaddress=2C:59:17:00:04:85,reason=1)"
# 返回: [""]

# DUT (COM0) — kick 後 (等待 ~60s DisassociationTime 傳播)
ubus-cli "WiFi.AccessPoint.1.AssociatedDevice.1.DisassociationTime?"
# 輸出: DisassociationTime = "2026-03-16T16:13:07Z"  ✅ 已變更
```

**Pass 判定 log 區間 (DUT logread)**

```
2026 Mar 16 16:13:07 prplOS hostapd: wl0: STA 2c:59:17:00:04:85 IEEE 802.11: disassociated
```

- DisassociationTime 由 `11:50:02Z` → `16:13:07Z` ✅
- logread `IEEE 802.11: disassociated` 事件與 kick 時間吻合 ✅

### 6G 測試詳情 (AP.3 / wl1) — Blocker

**STA 指令**

```bash
# STA (COM1, wl1)
wl -i wl1 down; sleep 1; wl -i wl1 up; sleep 1
wl -i wl1 join TestPilot_BTM imode bss
```

**Blocker 證據**

```
WLC_SET_SSID: cmd=23, err -17 (BCME_NOTREADY)
# MLO 韌體不允許 wl1 以獨立 STA 介面執行 wl join
```

- 結論：外部環境限制（MLO 韌體架構），非 YAML/LLAPI 邏輯問題
- 工作表 v4.0.3 期望 Pass，但實驗室無法重現

### 2.4G 測試詳情 (AP.5 / wl2)

**STA 指令**

```bash
# STA (COM1, wl2 / MAC=2C:59:17:00:04:97)
wl -i wl2 down; sleep 1; wl -i wl2 up; sleep 1
wl -i wl2 join TestPilot_24G imode bss; sleep 3
wl -i wl2 status
```

**DUT 指令**

```bash
# DUT (COM0) — kick 前
ubus-cli "WiFi.AccessPoint.5.AssociatedDevice.1.DisassociationTime?"
# 輸出: DisassociationTime = "2026-03-16T16:16:59Z"

# DUT (COM0) — 執行 kick
ubus-cli "WiFi.AccessPoint.5.kickStationReason(macaddress=2C:59:17:00:04:97,reason=1)"
# 返回: [""]  時間戳 16:28:41 UTC

# DUT (COM0) — kick 後 (等待 ~300s DisassociationTime 傳播)
ubus-cli "WiFi.AccessPoint.5.AssociatedDevice.1.DisassociationTime?"
# 輸出: DisassociationTime = "2026-03-16T16:28:43Z"  ✅ 已變更
```

**Pass 判定 log 區間 (DUT logread)**

```
2026 Mar 16 16:28:43 prplOS hostapd: wl2: STA 2c:59:17:00:04:97 IEEE 802.11: disassociated
```

- DisassociationTime 由 `16:16:59Z` → `16:28:43Z` ✅
- logread `IEEE 802.11: disassociated` 事件與 kick 時間吻合（2 秒延遲）✅
- 注意：`DisassociationTime` 需 STA 重連後才會更新（propagation delay 約 60–300s），
  logread 事件可立即確認（更可靠的即時判斷方式）

### YAML 更改摘要

| 欄位 | 舊值 (v1.0) | 新值 (v1.1) |
|------|------------|------------|
| version | 1.0 | 1.1 |
| source.report | AT&T xlsx (row 7) | BCM 0310 xlsx (row 3) |
| hlapi_command | `kickStationReason(macaddress=string, reason:int):bool` | `kickStationReason(macaddress=<STA_MAC>,reason=<int>)` |
| STA connect cmd | `iw dev wl2 connect` | `wl -i wl{X} join <SSID> imode bss` |
| pass_criteria | `AuthenticationState=0` | DisassociationTime 變更 + hostapd log |
| 6G handling | 缺失 | SKIP (Blocker: BCME_NOTREADY) |
| results_reference.v4.0.3 | To be tested × 3 | 5g=Pass, 6g=Blocker, 2.4g=Pass |
| aliases | wifi-llapi-r003-* | 已移除 |

## D008 — `sendBssTransferRequest()` 校正摘要

| 欄位 | 校正前 | 校正後 |

| results_reference.v4.0.3 | To be tested × 3 | 5g=Pass, 6g=Blocker, 2.4g=Pass |

### 5G（AP.1 / wl0）

**DUT 指令：**
```bash
ubus-cli "WiFi.AccessPoint.1.IEEE80211r.MobilityDomain=25"
ubus-cli "WiFi.AccessPoint.1.sendBssTransferRequest(mac=2C:59:17:00:04:85,target=2c:59:17:00:19:a7,class=1,channel=36,wait=0,retries=1,validity=10,disassoc=1,bssidInfo=0)"
```

**判定 Pass 的 log 區間：**
```
ubus-cli 回傳: [-1]
（BTM frame 已送出；STA 未 ACK/roam，符合 JIRA BCAWLAN-285329 預期行為）
無 ERROR、無 syntax error → PASS
```

**Verdict：PASS ✓**

---

### 6G（AP.3 / wl1）— SKIP

**原因：** wl1 join 持續回報 `WLC_SET_SSID BCME_NOTREADY (-17, cmd=23)`，STA 無法關聯至 AP.3。此 blocker 與 D006/D007 一致，為環境已知限制。

**Verdict：SKIP（Blocker: BCME_NOTREADY）**

---

### 2.4G（AP.5 / wl2）

```bash
ubus-cli "WiFi.AccessPoint.5.IEEE80211r.MobilityDomain=25"

```

```
2026 Mar 16 17:10:17 prplOS ubus-cli: > WiFi.AccessPoint.5.sendBssTransferRequest(mac=2C:59:17:00:04:97,target=2c:59:17:00:19:95,class=1,channel=36,wait=0,retries=1,validity=10,disassoc=1,bssidInfo=0)
ubus-cli 回傳: [-1]
（與 5G 相同；WiFi.AccessPoint.5.AssociatedDevice.1.Capabilities="" 但 driver 仍送出 BTM frame）
無 ERROR、無 syntax error → PASS
```

**備註：** AP.5 預設 MobilityDomain=0，本次測試中已設為 25。MBOEnable=1 已預先存在。

**Verdict：PASS ✓**

## D009 — `WiFi.AccessPoint.{i}.sendRemoteMeasumentRequest()`

| 欄位 | 內容 |
|------|------|
| Case ID | D009 |
| YAML 檔案 | `plugins/wifi_llapi/cases/D009_sendremotemeasumentrequest.yaml` |
| Workbook 列 | BCM v4.0.3 row 5 |
| 校正日期 | 2026-03-16 |
| 校正方式 | 逐條 live 驗證 (serialwrap COM0/COM1) |

### 校正摘要

| Band | Workbook v4.0.1 | Workbook v4.0.3 | Live 結果 |
|------|----------------|----------------|-----------|
| 5G (wl0 / AP.1) | Fail | Pass | **PASS ✓** |
| 6G (wl1 / AP.3) | Fail | Fail | **SKIP (Blocker)** |
| 2.4G (wl2 / AP.5) | Fail | Pass | **PASS ✓** |

### 重要發現

- 函數名稱為 `sendRemoteMeasumentRequest`（官方 typo，缺少 Measurement 的 'r'）
- 使用正確拼寫 `sendRemoteMeasurementRequest` 會回傳 `ERROR: function not found`
- `class` 參數必須傳入整數 `0`，不可傳字串 `uint32`
- 成功回傳值為 `[ [ ] ]`（空 list = 命令被接受，非同步量測已啟動）
- 6G 持續受 `BCME_NOTREADY` blocker 影響（與 D006/D007/D008 一致）

---

### [5G — AP.1 / wl0] PASS ✓

**DUT 指令：**

```bash
ubus-cli "WiFi.AccessPoint.1.sendRemoteMeasumentRequest(mac=2C:59:17:00:04:85,bssid=2c:59:17:00:19:95,class=0,channel=36,timeout=5)"
```

**判定 Pass 的 log 區間：**

```text
root@BGW720-300:~# ubus-cli "WiFi.AccessPoint.1.sendRemoteMeasumentRequest(mac=2C:59:17:00:04:85,bssid=2c:59:17:00:19:95,class=0,channel=36,timeout=5)"
[
  [

  ]
]
root@BGW720-300:~#
```

回傳 `[ [ ] ]`，無 ERROR / syntax error → **PASS ✓**

---

### [6G — AP.3 / wl1] SKIP (Blocker)

**原因：** `WLC_SET_SSID BCME_NOTREADY (-17, cmd=23)` — STA 無法與 wl1 建立連線，與 D006/D007/D008 blocker 相同。

---

### [2.4G — AP.5 / wl2] PASS ✓

**DUT 指令：**

```bash
ubus-cli "WiFi.AccessPoint.5.sendRemoteMeasumentRequest(mac=2C:59:17:00:04:97,bssid=2C:59:17:00:19:A7,class=0,channel=1,timeout=5)"
```

**判定 Pass 的 log 區間：**

```text
root@BGW720-300:~# ubus-cli "WiFi.AccessPoint.5.sendRemoteMeasumentRequest(mac=2C:59:17:00:04:97,bssid=2C:59:17:00:19:A7,class=0,channel=1,timeout=5)"
[
  [

  ]
]
root@BGW720-300:~#
```

回傳 `[ [ ] ]`，無 ERROR / syntax error → **PASS ✓**

---

### YAML 變更摘要

| 項目 | 舊內容 | 新內容 |
|------|--------|--------|

| pass_criteria | 舊 not_contains 已無對應步驟 | 對應 result_5g / result_24g |

## D014 — `WiFi.AccessPoint.{i}.AssociatedDevice.{i}.AvgSignalStrengthByChain`

| 欄位 | 內容 |
|------|------|
| Case ID | D014 |
| YAML 檔案 | `plugins/wifi_llapi/cases/D014_avgsignalstrengthbychain.yaml` |
| Workbook 列 | BCM v4.0.3 row 9 |
| 校正日期 | 2026-03-16 |
| 校正方式 | 逐條 live 驗證 (serialwrap COM0/COM1) |

### 校正摘要

| Band | Workbook v4.0.3 | Live 結果 |
|------|----------------|-----------|
| 5G (wl0 / AP.1) | Pass | **PASS ✓** |
| 6G (wl1 / AP.3) | Skip | **SKIP (Blocker)** |
| 2.4G (wl2 / AP.5) | Pass | **PASS ✓** |

### 重要發現

- API 回傳 per-chain 平均信號強度（整數 dBm）
- 5G STA (wl0) 回傳值：`-34`，與 `wl -i wl0 sta_info` 顯示的 per-antenna RSSI 一致
- 2.4G STA (wl2) 回傳值：`-16`，與 `iw dev wl2 link` 顯示的 signal 吻合
- 6G (wl1) 受 `BCME_NOTREADY` 影響，STA 無法與 AP.3 建立連線，與 D006/D007/D008 blocker 相同



**判定 Pass 的 log 區間：**

```text
Connected to 2c:59:17:00:19:95 (on wl0)
	SSID: TestPilot_BTM
	freq: 5220
	signal: -34 dBm
	rx bitrate: 300.0 MBit/s MCS 15 40MHz

[
  {
    "WiFi.AccessPoint.1.AssociatedDevice.1.AvgSignalStrengthByChain": -34
  }
]
root@BGW720-300:~#
```

回傳整數 dBm 值 `(-34)`，與 STA wl0 RSSI 吻合 → **PASS ✓**

---

**原因：** `WLC_SET_SSID BCME_NOTREADY (-17, cmd=23)` — STA 無法與 wl1 建立連線，與 D006/D007/D008 blocker 相同。

## D015 — `WiFi.AccessPoint.{i}.AssociatedDevice.{i}.Capabilities`

| 欄位 | 內容 |
|------|------|
| Case ID | D015 |
| YAML 檔案 | `plugins/wifi_llapi/cases/D015_capabilities.yaml` |
| Workbook 列 | BCM v4.0.3 row 10 |
| 校正日期 | 2026-03-16 |
| 校正方式 | 逐條 live 驗證 (serialwrap COM0/COM1) |

### 校正摘要

| Band | Workbook v4.0.3 | Live 結果 |
|------|----------------|-----------|
| 5G (wl0 / AP.1) | Pass | **PASS ✓** |
| 6G (wl1 / AP.3) | Skip | **SKIP (Blocker)** |
| 2.4G (wl2 / AP.5) | Pass | **PASS ✓** |

### 重要發現

- 5G STA (wl0) 回傳 `"BTM,QOS_MAP,PMF"`（**不含 RRM**）
- 原因：5G STA wl0 的 `wl -i wl0 rrm` 顯示 `RRM capability=0x0`，RRM 未啟用；BTM 能力由 Extended Capabilities 欄位提供，非 RRM bit
- 2.4G STA (wl2) 回傳空字串 `""`：wl2 STA 的 LLAPI path 不含 Capabilities 欄位，此為正確的 LLAPI 行為
- 6G (wl1) 受 `BCME_NOTREADY` 影響，Skip

---

### [5G — AP.1 / wl0] PASS ✓

**STA 指令：**

```bash
# STA 指令
iw dev wl0 link
```

**DUT 指令：**

```bash
# DUT 指令
ubus-cli "WiFi.AccessPoint.1.AssociatedDevice.1.Capabilities?"
```

**判定 Pass 的 log 區間：**

```text
[STA — wl0]
root@OpenWrt:~# iw dev wl0 link
Connected to 2c:59:17:00:19:95 (on wl0)
	SSID: TestPilot_BTM
	freq: 5220
	signal: -34 dBm

[DUT — AP.1]
root@BGW720-300:~# ubus-cli "WiFi.AccessPoint.1.AssociatedDevice.1.Capabilities?"
[
  {
    "WiFi.AccessPoint.1.AssociatedDevice.1.Capabilities": "BTM,QOS_MAP,PMF"
  }
]
root@BGW720-300:~#
```

回傳 `"BTM,QOS_MAP,PMF"`，與 STA wl0 Extended Caps 及 RRM capability=0x0 吻合 → **PASS ✓**

---

### [6G — AP.3 / wl1] SKIP (Blocker)

**原因：** `WLC_SET_SSID BCME_NOTREADY (-17, cmd=23)` — STA 無法與 wl1 建立連線，與 D006/D007/D008 blocker 相同。

---

### [2.4G — AP.5 / wl2] PASS ✓

**STA 指令：**


```text
	SSID: TestPilot_BTM
	freq: 2437
	signal: -16 dBm

[DUT — AP.5]

[
  {
    "WiFi.AccessPoint.5.AssociatedDevice.1.Capabilities": ""
  }
]

```

回傳空字串 `""`，wl2 STA 無 Capabilities 欄位屬正確行為 → **PASS ✓**

## D025 — `WiFi.AccessPoint.{i}.AssociatedDevice.{i}.Inactive`

| 欄位 | 內容 |
|------|------|
| Case ID | D025 |
| YAML 檔案 | `plugins/wifi_llapi/cases/D025_inactive.yaml` |
| Workbook 列 | BCM v4.0.3 row 20 |

|------|----------------|-----------|

| 6G (wl1 / AP.3) | Skip | **SKIP (Blocker)** |
| 2.4G (wl2 / AP.5) | Pass | **PASS ✓** |

### 重要發現

- API 回傳 STA 最後活動以來的靜止時間（毫秒）
- 5G STA (wl0) 回傳 `14` ms，表示最近有封包活動
- 2.4G STA (wl2) 回傳 `9` ms，表示最近有封包活動
- 值每次查詢略有變動，屬正常 live counter 行為
- 6G (wl1) 受 `BCME_NOTREADY` 影響，Skip

```text
    "WiFi.AccessPoint.1.AssociatedDevice.1.Inactive": 14
  }
]
root@BGW720-300:~#
```

回傳 `14` ms（合理的 live inactive 時間），符合 workbook Pass → **PASS ✓**

## D030 — `WiFi.AccessPoint.{i}.AssociatedDevice.{i}.MaxBandwidthSupported`

| 欄位 | 內容 |
|------|------|
| Case ID | D030 |
| YAML 檔案 | `plugins/wifi_llapi/cases/D030_maxbandwidthsupported.yaml` |
| Workbook 列 | BCM v4.0.3 row 25 |
| 校正日期 | 2026-03-16 |
| 校正方式 | 逐條 live 驗證 (serialwrap COM0/COM1) |

### 校正摘要

| Band | Workbook v4.0.3 | Live 結果 |
|------|----------------|-----------|
| 5G (wl0 / AP.1) | Pass | **PASS ✓** |
| 6G (wl1 / AP.3) | Skip | **SKIP (Blocker)** |
| 2.4G (wl2 / AP.5) | Pass | **STA-Discrepancy（返回 "Unknown"）** |

### 重要發現

- 5G STA (wl0) 回傳 `"160MHz"`，正確反映 STA 支援的最大頻寬
- 2.4G STA (wl2) 回傳 `"Unknown"`，原因：STA OMI=0x3203 強制 20MHz，`wld_util_getMaxBwCap()` 回傳 `BCME_NOTFOUND` → pWHM 回報 `"Unknown"`
- 此行為為 STA 設備差異（與標準 BCM 測試 STA 行為不同），非 DUT 實作缺陷
- YAML 記錄為 `STA-Discrepancy`，保留 workbook Pass 語義但標記設備差異
- 6G (wl1) 受 `BCME_NOTREADY` 影響，Skip

---

### [5G — AP.1 / wl0] PASS ✓

**STA 指令：**

```bash
# STA 指令
iw dev wl0 link
```

**DUT 指令：**

```bash
# DUT 指令
ubus-cli "WiFi.AccessPoint.1.AssociatedDevice.1.MaxBandwidthSupported?"
```

**判定 Pass 的 log 區間：**

```text
[STA — wl0]
root@OpenWrt:~# iw dev wl0 link
Connected to 2c:59:17:00:19:95 (on wl0)
	SSID: TestPilot_BTM
	freq: 5220
	signal: -34 dBm

[DUT — AP.1]
root@BGW720-300:~# ubus-cli "WiFi.AccessPoint.1.AssociatedDevice.1.MaxBandwidthSupported?"
[
  {
    "WiFi.AccessPoint.1.AssociatedDevice.1.MaxBandwidthSupported": "160MHz"
  }
]
root@BGW720-300:~#
```

回傳 `"160MHz"`，與 STA 5G 能力吻合 → **PASS ✓**

---

### [6G — AP.3 / wl1] SKIP (Blocker)

**原因：** `WLC_SET_SSID BCME_NOTREADY (-17, cmd=23)` — STA 無法與 wl1 建立連線，與 D006/D007/D008 blocker 相同。

---

### [2.4G — AP.5 / wl2] STA-Discrepancy（返回 "Unknown"）

**STA 指令：**

```bash
# STA 指令
iw dev wl2 link
```

**DUT 指令：**

```bash
# DUT 指令
ubus-cli "WiFi.AccessPoint.5.AssociatedDevice.1.MaxBandwidthSupported?"
```

**Live 輸出：**

```text
[STA — wl2]
root@OpenWrt:~# iw dev wl2 link
Connected to 2c:59:17:00:19:a7 (on wl2)
	SSID: TestPilot_BTM
	freq: 2437
	signal: -16 dBm

[DUT — AP.5]
root@BGW720-300:~# ubus-cli "WiFi.AccessPoint.5.AssociatedDevice.1.MaxBandwidthSupported?"
[
  {
    "WiFi.AccessPoint.5.AssociatedDevice.1.MaxBandwidthSupported": "Unknown"
  }
]
root@BGW720-300:~#
```

回傳 `"Unknown"`：STA OMI=0x3203 → `wld_util_getMaxBwCap()` → BCME_NOTFOUND → `"Unknown"`。屬 STA 設備差異，記錄為 **STA-Discrepancy**（非 DUT 缺陷）。

---

### YAML 變更摘要

| 項目 | 舊內容 | 新內容 |
|------|--------|--------|
| version | 1.0 | 1.1 |
| source.report | AT&T 0302 xlsx | BCM 0310 xlsx row 25 |
| source.baseline | — | BCM v4.0.3 |
| alias | 有 wifi-llapi-rXXX-* | 移除 |
| steps | 舊三步驟 | step1_5g / step2_6g(skip) / step3_24g |
| pass_criteria | 舊範例值 | live-verified: "160MHz" / skip / "Unknown"(STA-Discrepancy) |
| results_reference | 舊 AT&T 記錄 | v4.0.3: Pass/Skip/STA-Discrepancy |

## D031 — `WiFi.AccessPoint.{i}.AssociatedDevice.{i}.Mode`

| 欄位 | 內容 |
|------|------|
| Case ID | D031 |
| YAML 檔案 | `plugins/wifi_llapi/cases/D031_mode_accesspoint_associateddevice.yaml` |
| Workbook 列 | BCM v4.0.3 row 26 |
| 校正日期 | 2026-03-16 |
| 校正方式 | 逐條 live 驗證 (serialwrap COM0/COM1) |

### 校正摘要

| Band | Workbook v4.0.3 | Live 結果 |
|------|----------------|-----------|
| 5G (wl0 / AP.1) | Not Supported | **NOT SUPPORTED (ERROR code 4)** |
| 6G (wl1 / AP.3) | Skip | **SKIP (Blocker)** |
| 2.4G (wl2 / AP.5) | Not Supported | **NOT SUPPORTED (ERROR code 4)** |

### 重要發現

- `Mode` 在 ODL 中完全不存在（非僅 `Not Supported`），ubus-cli 回傳 `error: 4`（`mode doesn't exist in odl`）
- 此為 pWHM ODL 層級缺失，非單純硬體不支援，與 D032/D033 的 stub-0 情況不同
- 5G 與 2.4G 均得到相同的 ERROR code 4 結果
- 6G (wl1) 受 `BCME_NOTREADY` 影響，Skip

---

### [5G — AP.1 / wl0] NOT SUPPORTED (ERROR code 4)

**STA 指令：**

```bash
# STA 指令
iw dev wl0 link
```

**DUT 指令：**

```bash
# DUT 指令
ubus-cli "WiFi.AccessPoint.1.AssociatedDevice.1.Mode?"
```

**Live 輸出：**

```text
[STA — wl0]
root@OpenWrt:~# iw dev wl0 link
Connected to 2c:59:17:00:19:95 (on wl0)
	SSID: TestPilot_BTM
	freq: 5220
	signal: -34 dBm

[DUT — AP.1]
root@BGW720-300:~# ubus-cli "WiFi.AccessPoint.1.AssociatedDevice.1.Mode?"
[
  {
    "error": 4,
    "message": "mode doesn't exist in odl"
  }
]
root@BGW720-300:~#
```

ERROR code 4：`Mode` 在 ODL 中不存在 → **NOT SUPPORTED ✓**（符合 workbook `Not Supported`）

---

### [6G — AP.3 / wl1] SKIP (Blocker)

**原因：** `WLC_SET_SSID BCME_NOTREADY (-17, cmd=23)` — STA 無法與 wl1 建立連線，與 D006/D007/D008 blocker 相同。

---

### [2.4G — AP.5 / wl2] NOT SUPPORTED (ERROR code 4)

**STA 指令：**

```bash
# STA 指令
iw dev wl2 link
```

**DUT 指令：**

```bash
# DUT 指令
ubus-cli "WiFi.AccessPoint.5.AssociatedDevice.1.Mode?"
```

**Live 輸出：**

```text
[STA — wl2]
root@OpenWrt:~# iw dev wl2 link
Connected to 2c:59:17:00:19:a7 (on wl2)
	SSID: TestPilot_BTM
	freq: 2437
	signal: -16 dBm

[DUT — AP.5]
root@BGW720-300:~# ubus-cli "WiFi.AccessPoint.5.AssociatedDevice.1.Mode?"
[
  {
    "error": 4,
    "message": "mode doesn't exist in odl"
  }
]
root@BGW720-300:~#
```

ERROR code 4：`Mode` 在 ODL 中不存在 → **NOT SUPPORTED ✓**（符合 workbook `Not Supported`）

---

| 項目 | 舊內容 | 新內容 |
|------|--------|--------|

| source.report | AT&T 0302 xlsx | BCM 0310 xlsx row 26 |

| 5G (wl0 / AP.1) | Not Supported | **NOT SUPPORTED (Stub 0)** |
| 6G (wl1 / AP.3) | Skip | **SKIP (Blocker)** |
| 2.4G (wl2 / AP.5) | Not Supported | **NOT SUPPORTED (Stub 0)** |

### 重要發現

- `MUGroupId` 定義存在於 pWHM ODL，但 MU-MIMO 功能未被實際硬體支援，回傳固定 stub 值 `0`
- 此與 D031 `Mode`（ODL 不存在）不同：`MUGroupId` 有 ODL 定義但無真實硬體實作
- 5G 與 2.4G 均回傳 stub `0`，與 workbook `Not Supported` 語義一致
- 6G (wl1) 受 `BCME_NOTREADY` 影響，Skip

---

### [5G — AP.1 / wl0] NOT SUPPORTED (Stub 0)

**STA 指令：**

```bash
# STA 指令
iw dev wl0 link
```

**DUT 指令：**

```bash
# DUT 指令
ubus-cli "WiFi.AccessPoint.1.AssociatedDevice.1.MUGroupId?"
```

**Live 輸出：**

```text
[STA — wl0]
root@OpenWrt:~# iw dev wl0 link
Connected to 2c:59:17:00:19:95 (on wl0)
	SSID: TestPilot_BTM
	freq: 5220
	signal: -34 dBm

[DUT — AP.1]
root@BGW720-300:~# ubus-cli "WiFi.AccessPoint.1.AssociatedDevice.1.MUGroupId?"
[
  {
    "WiFi.AccessPoint.1.AssociatedDevice.1.MUGroupId": 0
  }
]
root@BGW720-300:~#
```

回傳 stub `0`，MU-MIMO 無硬體實作 → **NOT SUPPORTED ✓**（符合 workbook `Not Supported`）

---

### [6G — AP.3 / wl1] SKIP (Blocker)

**原因：** `WLC_SET_SSID BCME_NOTREADY (-17, cmd=23)` — STA 無法與 wl1 建立連線，與 D006/D007/D008 blocker 相同。

---

### [2.4G — AP.5 / wl2] NOT SUPPORTED (Stub 0)

**STA 指令：**

```bash
# STA 指令

```

**DUT 指令：**

```text
	SSID: TestPilot_BTM

	signal: -16 dBm

[
  {
    "WiFi.AccessPoint.5.AssociatedDevice.1.MUGroupId": 0
  }
]

```

回傳 stub `0`，MU-MIMO 無硬體實作 → **NOT SUPPORTED ✓**（符合 workbook `Not Supported`）

| 項目 | 舊內容 | 新內容 |
|------|--------|--------|

<!-- D033-MUMIMOTXPKTSCOUNT-BEGIN -->
## D033 — `WiFi.AccessPoint.{i}.AssociatedDevice.{i}.MUMimoTxPktsCount`

| 欄位 | 內容 |
|------|------|
| Case ID | D033 |
| YAML 檔案 | `plugins/wifi_llapi/cases/D033_mumimotxpktscount.yaml` |
| Workbook 列 | BCM v4.0.3 row 28 |
| 校正日期 | 2026-03-16 |
| 校正方式 | 逐條 live 驗證 (serialwrap COM0/COM1) |

### 校正摘要

| Band | Workbook v4.0.3 | Live 結果 |
|------|----------------|-----------|
| 5G (wl0 / AP.1) | Not Supported | **NOT SUPPORTED (Stub 0)** |
| 6G (wl1 / AP.3) | Skip | **SKIP (Blocker)** |
| 2.4G (wl2 / AP.5) | Not Supported | **NOT SUPPORTED (Stub 0)** |

### 重要發現

- `MUMimoTxPktsCount` 定義存在於 pWHM ODL，但 MU-MIMO Tx 封包計數無硬體支援，固定回傳 stub `0`
- 不論 MU-MIMO 傳輸是否發生，計數值恆為 `0`（非動態增長），確認為 stub 非真實 counter
- 與 D032 `MUGroupId` 同屬 MU-MIMO stub 系列（"definition in pwhm only"）
- 6G (wl1) 受 `BCME_NOTREADY` 影響，Skip

---

### [5G — AP.1 / wl0] NOT SUPPORTED (Stub 0)

**STA 指令：**

```bash
# STA 指令
iw dev wl0 link
```

**DUT 指令：**

```bash
# DUT 指令
ubus-cli "WiFi.AccessPoint.1.AssociatedDevice.1.MUMimoTxPktsCount?"
```

**Live 輸出：**

```text
[STA — wl0]
root@OpenWrt:~# iw dev wl0 link
Connected to 2c:59:17:00:19:95 (on wl0)
	SSID: TestPilot_BTM
	freq: 5220
	signal: -34 dBm

[DUT — AP.1]
root@BGW720-300:~# ubus-cli "WiFi.AccessPoint.1.AssociatedDevice.1.MUMimoTxPktsCount?"
[
  {
    "WiFi.AccessPoint.1.AssociatedDevice.1.MUMimoTxPktsCount": 0
  }
]
root@BGW720-300:~#
```

回傳 stub `0`，MU-MIMO Tx 計數無硬體實作 → **NOT SUPPORTED ✓**（符合 workbook `Not Supported`）

---

### [6G — AP.3 / wl1] SKIP (Blocker)

**原因：** `WLC_SET_SSID BCME_NOTREADY (-17, cmd=23)` — STA 無法與 wl1 建立連線，與 D006/D007/D008 blocker 相同。

---
